---------Deviation in Simplefied KYC start-----25-8-2022------- 
  
create table loc_ash_simpl_kyc as select distinct c.cust_id,
       c.cust_name,
       d.reg_date,
       b.BRANCH_ID,
       b.BRANCH_NAME,
       b.area_name,
       b.reg_name,
       f.fzm,
       (case 
         when p.kyc_photo is null then
          'NO KYC'
         else
          'KYC'
       end) KYC_PHOTO_STS,
       (case 
       when p.pledge_photo is null then
         'NO CUSTOMER_PHOTO' 
         else 
           'CUSTOMER PHOTO'
            end) customer_photo_sts
      
       from mana0809.customer c, 
       mana0809.customer_detail d, 
       mana0809.customer_photo p, 
       mana0809.branch_dtl_new b, 
       mana0809.tbl_fzm_master f 
       where c.cust_id = d.cust_id 
       and c.cust_id = p.cust_id 
       and c.branch_id = b.BRANCH_ID
       and b.reg_id = f.region_id;
       
   --------------------------------------------------------------------
     
merge into loc_ash_simpl_kyc x
using (select T.CUST_ID,
              D.ID_NUMBER,
              I.IDENTITY_NAME,
              I.IDENTITY_ID,
              D.ISSUE_DT,
              D.EXP_DT
         from loc_ash_simpl_kyc     t,
              mana0809.identity_dtl d,
              mana0809.identity     i
        where t.cust_id = d.cust_id
          and d.identity_id = i.identity_id) y
on (x.cust_id = y.cust_id)
when matched then
  update
     set X.IDENTITY_NO   = Y.ID_NUMBER,
         X.IDENTITY_NAME = Y.IDENTITY_NAME,
         X.IDENTITY_ID   = Y.IDENTITY_ID,
         X.ISSUE_DATE    = Y.ISSUE_DT,
         X.EXP_DATE      = Y.EXP_DT;
         
         COMMIT;
         
         
    -------------------------------------------------------     
         
         merge into loc_ash_simpl_kyc x
using (select T.CUST_ID,
            d.pan
         from loc_ash_simpl_kyc     t,
         dms.deposit_pan_detail d
        where t.cust_id = d.cust_id) y
on (x.cust_id = y.cust_id)
when matched then
  update
     set x.pan_no=y.pan;
     
     COMMIT;
     
     
 ---------------------------------------------------------------
 
     merge into loc_ash_simpl_kyc x
using (select t.cust_id,d.kyc_adhar_status
         from loc_ash_simpl_kyc     t,
         mana0809.customer_photo d
        where t.cust_id = d.cust_id) y
on (x.cust_id = y.cust_id)
when matched then
  update
     set x.Kyc_Adhar_Status=y.Kyc_Adhar_Status;
     
     COMMIT;
     
 -----------------------------------------------------------------
 
 --PAN_STS---
 update loc_ash_simpl_kyc t set t.pan_sts='Yes' 
 where exists(select distinct cust_id from (select t.cust_id,t.pan from mana0809.customer_detail t
where t.pan is not null

union all

select d.cust_id,d.pan from dms.deposit_pan_detail d
where d.pan is not null) h
where t.cust_id=h.cust_id );
commit;

update loc_ash_simpl_kyc t set t.pan_sts='No' where t.pan_sts is null;
commit;


---------------------------------------------------------------------



     
    merge into loc_ash_simpl_kyc x
using   (select p.CUST_ID,max(p.PLEDGE_VAL)max_pledge_val  from mana0809.full_pledge_master p,loc_ash_simpl_kyc t
where p.cust_id=t.cust_id group by p.CUST_ID) y on (x.cust_id = y.cust_id)
when matched then
  update
     set x.max_pledge_val=y.max_pledge_val;
     
     COMMIT;
     
     
------FORM 60 STS----

 update loc_ash_simpl_kyc t set t.form60_sts='Yes' 
 where exists(select distinct cust_id from (select to_char(t.customer_id) cust_id from mana0809.tbl_online_pan_details t
union all
select to_char(h.customer_id) cust_id from mana0809.tbl_online_pan_details_his h
union all
select d.cust_id from dms.tbl_customer_form60 d
where d.form_60 is not null) p
where t.cust_id=p.cust_id );
COMMIT;

update loc_ash_simpl_kyc t set t.form60_sts='No' where t.form60_sts is null;
COMMIT;

create table sim_kyc_data as select distinct t.*,c.outstanding_amt,c.Total_credit
  from loc_ash_simpl_kyc t, tableau_er1 d,
  (select z.cust_id,sum(z.balance) outstanding_amt,(sum(z.pledge_amount)+sum(z.amount)) Total_credit from tableau_er1 z
  group by z.cust_id) c
 where t.cust_id = d.cust_id
   and t.cust_id=c.cust_id
   and d.cus_status = 'Full KYC'
   and ((t.identity_id not in
       (502, 2, 552, 503, 1, 553, 16, 555, 505, 501, 3, 551, 17, 18)) or
       (t.customer_photo_sts='NO CUSTOMER_PHOTO') or
       (t.pan_sts = 'No' and t.form60_sts = 'No'));

select  d.cust_name,tt.gender,tt.date_of_birth,p.id_number ,count(p.id_number ) cnt  from
  customer_detail   tt,  identity_dtl  p, customer  d ,(select  a.cust_name,count(t.id_number)
         from    identity_dtl   t, customer  a,(select distinct j.id_number ,j.cust_id  from kl j) jj
        where t.identity_id =16 and a.cust_id=t.cust_id and a.isactive=1 and jj.id_number=t.id_number group by a.cust_name 
        having count(t.id_number)>1) x where  d.cust_id=tt.cust_id and  d.cust_name=x.cust_name

         from   mana0809.identity_dtl@uatr_backup2  t,mana0809.customer@uatr_backup2 a,kl j
        where t.identity_id =2 and a.cust_id=t.cust_id and a.isactive=1 and j.id_number=t.id_number group by a.cust_name

select a.branch_id,a.cust_name,a.isactive,a.cust_id,b.reg_date,b.date_of_birth,b.gender,c.id_number,c.identity_id from customer a,customer_detail b,identity_dtl c where c.cust_id=a.cust_id and  b.cust_id = a.cust_id and (a.cust_name,b.date_of_birth,b.gender,c.id_number) in(
select t.cust_name,t.date_of_birth,t.gender,t.id_number from multiple_cust_vv t) order by c.id_number

create table mustiple_cust_id_aadhar as select  d.cust_name,tt.gender,tt.date_of_birth,p.id_number ,count(p.id_number ) cnt from
 mana0809.customer_detail@uatr_backup2  tt, mana0809.identity_dtl@uatr_backup2  p,mana0809.customer@uatr_backup2 d ,(select  a.cust_name,count(t.id_number)
         from   mana0809.identity_dtl@uatr_backup2  t,mana0809.customer@uatr_backup2 a
        where t.identity_id =16 and a.cust_id=t.cust_id and a.isactive=1 group by a.cust_name 
        having count(t.id_number)>1) x where d.cust_id=tt.cust_id and  d.cust_name=x.cust_name 
        and p.identity_id=16 and tt.cust_id=p.cust_id and d.isactive=1
          group by d.cust_name,tt.gender,tt.date_of_birth,p.id_number having count(p.id_number )>1;


select a.branch_id,a.cust_name,a.isactive,a.cust_id,b.reg_date,b.gender,c.id_number,c.identity_id from customer a,customer_detail b,identity_dtl c where c.cust_id=a.cust_id and  b.cust_id = a.cust_id and (a.cust_name,b.date_of_birth,b.gender,c.id_number) in(
select t.cust_name,t.date_of_birth,t.gender,t.id_number from MUSTIPLE_CUST_ID_AADHAR t) order by c.id_number

create table customer_category_vv as 
SLNO#25 RBI observation checking query 13-Aug-2022
select /*+append parallel(10)*/
        *
        from (select  to_char(p.cust_id)cust_id , to_char(p.cust_name) cust_name,
                     to_char(p.Risks)Risks , to_char(p.reg_date)reg_date ,
                     to_char(p.branch_id)branch_id , to_char(p.Category) Category,
                     to_char(p.rnum) rnum
                from (select rg.cust_id,rg.cust_name,rg.Risks,rg.reg_date,rg.branch_id,rg.Category,
                rownum rnum from (select distinct t.cust_id, c.cust_name,
                r.Risks,
                cd.reg_date,
                c.branch_id,
                decode(min(t.risk_type),
                       1,
                       'High Risk Category',
                       2,
                       'Medium Risk Category',
                       3,
                       'Low Risk Category') Category
  from MANA0809.tbl_cust_glm_classification@UATR_BACKUP2 t,
       mana0809.customer@UATR_BACKUP2                     c,
       mana0809.customer_detail@UATR_BACKUP2              cd,
        mana0809.CUSTOMER_RISK@UATR_BACKUP2                r,
      (select distinct k.cust_id from mana0809.tbl_pledge_yesterday_live@UATR_BACKUP2    k) y
   where t.cust_id = c.cust_id
   and t.cust_id = cd.cust_id
   and t.cust_id = r.cust_id
   and t.cust_id = y.cust_id
   and c.isactive = 1
   group by t.cust_id, c.cust_name,
                r.Risks,
                cd.reg_date,
                c.branch_id)rg)p
                 ---where p.rnum between 1 and  2000
                 order by p.rnum); -- max (page size * current page number)

CRF Tracker report for analysis 18-Jul-2022 from Anvito start

for getting crf content use this query: select a.Content_Data,a.* from dms.TBL_DRAFTMASTER_CONTENT@uatr_backup2 a where a.draft_no=107078
Step 1:
create table CRF_tracker_Report as select distinct t.note_id CRFID,decode(b.priority, 1, 'High', 2, 'Medium', 3,'Low') priority,e.request_id REQUESTID,b.note_id APPROVALID,to_char(b.tra_dt) REQUESTDATE,b.objective PROJECTNAME,c.EMP_NAME REQUESTEDBY,D.DEP_NAME USERDEPRTMENT,x.EMP_NAME TECHLEAD,e.tl_name TA_COMPLETEDBY,LISTAGG(g.EMP_NAME, ',') WITHIN GROUP(ORDER BY f.request_id) AS DEVELOPER,ep.EMP_NAME Code_reviewed_by,to_char(b.note_app_dt) MDAPPROVEDDATE, to_char(b.head_appr_date) HEADAPPROVED_DATE,to_char(b.target_dt) USER_TARGETDATE,to_char(s.tardt) TA_TARGETDATE, nvl(to_char(u.target_dt), to_char(s.tardt)) PROJECT_TARGET_DATE,to_char(u.revised_date) old_target_date,case when b.status_id in(99) then decode(b.status_id,99,'CRF CANCELLED BY USER')  when  nvl(upper(tt1.status), upper(t.status)) in ('CRF EDITED','TECHLEAD HANDOVER') then 'TA PENDING'  else  nvl(upper(tt1.status), upper(t.status)) end STATUS, case when (u.doc_update_sts=0 and (mana0809.business_hours_crf@uatr_backup2(wwl.received_date,sysdate,123))/8 > 3) then 'PENDING'  when u.doc_update_sts in(1,2,3,4) then 'IN PROGRESS'  when u.doc_update_sts=5 then 'COMPLETED' end RELEASE_DOCUMENTATION, to_char(wwl.received_date) RELEASE_DATE,nvl(e.development_manpower,xxy.Total_Work_Hours)Total_Work_Hours,yy.Module_Type 
  from mana0809.emp_master@uatr_backup2       c, mana0809.department_mst@uatr_backup2   d, mana0809.srm_draft_master@uatr_backup2 b
  LEFT OUTER JOIN MANA0809.srm_techlead_status@UATR_BACKUP2 E ON b.draft_no = E.DRAFT_NO
  left outer join (select p.note_id, p.request_id, max(p.updated_date) curr_status from (select * from mana0809.tbl_tracker_work_log@uatr_backup2 tb where tb.status not in  ('Documents Upload Pending','Code Review TA Completed','Code Review Completed','Documents Uploaded','Documents Reviewed by TechLead','Test case Updated','Document Review by TechLead Pending','Document Review by TechLead Pending','Developer Changed','TechLead Deleted','TechLead Changed','TechLead Added','Developer Deleted','TechLead Deleted','TechLead Changed','TechLead Added','Developer Deleted','TechLead Deleted','Initial Test Started')) p group by p.note_id, p.request_id) a  on a.note_id = to_char(b.draft_no)
  left outer join mana0809.srm_request_assign@uatr_backup2 f  on (f.request_id = e.request_id)
  left outer join mana0809.emp_master@uatr_backup2 g on g.EMP_CODE = f.assign_to
  left outer join mana0809.tbl_code_review@uatr_backup2 rv on rv.request_id=e.request_id
  left outer join mana0809.emp_master@uatr_backup2 ep on ep.EMP_CODE=rv.assign_to
  left outer join (select max(r.target_date) tardt, r.request_id from mana0809.srm_request_assign@uatr_backup2 r group by r.request_id) s on f.request_id = s.request_id
  left outer join mana0809.srm_software_request@uatr_backup2 u on b.draft_no = u.draft_id and e.request_id = u.request_id
  left outer join mana0809.TBL_TRACKER_WORK_LOG@uatr_backup2 t on to_char(b.draft_no) = to_char(t.note_id)
  left outer join mana0809.TBL_TRACKER_WORK_LOG@uatr_backup2 tt1 on tt1.note_id = to_char(b.draft_no) and tt1.request_id = u.request_id
  left outer join mana0809.SRM_TECH_TEAM_LEAD@uatr_backup2 v on u.it_team = v.team_id and v.tech_lead = 1
  left outer join mana0809.emp_master@uatr_backup2 x on x.EMP_CODE = v.emp_code
  left outer join (select distinct tm.type_id, tm.description as Module_Type from mana0809.srm_type_master@uatr_backup2  tm, mana0809.srm_draft_master@uatr_backup2 dm  where dm.module_type = tm.type_id) yy on yy.type_id = b.module_type
  left outer join (select a.request_id, sum(a.no_of_changes * a.cost_change) as Total_Work_Hours  from mana0809.srm_manpower_calculator@uatr_backup2 a group by a.request_id) xxy on xxy.request_id = e.request_id
  left outer join (select wl3.note_id, max(wl3.received_date) as rec_date  from mana0809.TBL_TRACKER_WORK_LOG@uatr_backup2 wl3 where wl3.sr_no = 2  and wl3.status = 'PMO Verification Pending'  group by wl3.note_id) wl2 on t.note_id = wl2.note_id
  left outer join (select ww.note_id, ww.received_date, ww.request_id  from mana0809.tbl_tracker_work_log@uatr_backup2 ww where ww.sr_no = 20) wwl on wwl.note_id = t.note_id and wwl.request_id = e.request_id 
 where a.note_id = t.note_id and a.curr_status = t.updated_date  and a.curr_status = tt1.updated_date and c.EMP_CODE = b.user_id and to_char(a.note_id) = to_char(b.draft_no) and b.dep_id = d.dep_id
  group by t.note_id,b.head_appr_date,e.request_id,e.development_manpower,ep.EMP_NAME,u.doc_update_sts,u.target_dt,b.priority,tt1.status,wwl.request_id,wwl.received_date,u.revised_date,b.note_id,b.tra_dt,b.objective,c.EMP_NAME,D.DEP_NAME,e.tl_name,b.note_app_dt,wl2.rec_date,b.target_dt,t.status,t.request_id,f.request_id,s.tardt,x.EMP_NAME,xxy.Total_Work_Hours,yy.Module_Type,b.status_id
union all (select distinct tt1.note_id CRFID,decode(b.priority, 1, 'High', 2, 'Medium', 3,'Low') priority,e.request_id REQUESTID, b.note_id APPROVALID,to_char(b.tra_dt) REQUESTDATE,b.objective PROJECTNAME,c.EMP_NAME REQUESTEDBY,D.DEP_NAME USERDEPRTMENT,x.EMP_NAME TECHLEAD,e.tl_name TA_COMPLETEDBY, LISTAGG(g.EMP_NAME, ',') WITHIN GROUP(ORDER BY f.request_id) AS DEVELOPER,ep.EMP_NAME Code_reviewed_by,to_char(b.note_app_dt) MDAPPROVEDDATE,to_char(b.head_appr_date) HEADAPPROVED_DATE,to_char(b.target_dt) USER_TARGETDATE,to_char(s.tardt) TA_TARGETDATE,nvl(to_char(u.target_dt), to_char(s.tardt)) PROJECT_TARGET_DATE,to_char(u.revised_date) old_target_date,case when b.status_id in(99) then decode(b.status_id,99,'CRF CANCELLED BY USER')  when  nvl(upper(tt1.status), upper(tt1.status)) in ('CRF EDITED','TECHLEAD HANDOVER') then 'TA PENDING'  else  nvl(upper(tt1.status), upper(tt1.status)) end STATUS, case when (u.doc_update_sts=0 and (mana0809.business_hours_crf@uatr_backup2(wwl.received_date,sysdate,123))/8 > 3) then 'PENDING'  when u.doc_update_sts in(1,2,3,4) then 'IN PROGRESS'  when u.doc_update_sts=5 then 'COMPLETED' end RELEASE_DOCUMENTATION,to_char(wwl.received_date) RELEASE_DATE,nvl(e.development_manpower,xxy.Total_Work_Hours)Total_Work_Hours,yy.Module_Type  from mana0809.emp_master@uatr_backup2       c, mana0809.department_mst@uatr_backup2   d, mana0809.srm_draft_master@uatr_backup2 b  LEFT OUTER JOIN MANA0809.srm_techlead_status@UATR_BACKUP2 E ON b.draft_no = E.DRAFT_NO left outer join (select p.note_id, max(p.updated_date) curr_status from (select * from mana0809.tbl_tracker_work_log@uatr_backup2 tb where tb.status not in('Documents Upload Pending','Code Review TA Completed','Code Review Completed','Documents Uploaded','Documents Reviewed by TechLead','Test case Updated','Document Review by TechLead Pending','Document Review by TechLead Pending','Developer Changed','TechLead Deleted','TechLead Changed','TechLead Added','Developer Deleted','TechLead Deleted','TechLead Changed','TechLead Added','Developer Deleted','TechLead Deleted','Initial Test Started') and tb.request_id is null and tb.note_id not in(select distinct  pp.note_id from (select *  from mana0809.tbl_tracker_work_log@uatr_backup2 tb1 where tb1.status not in('Documents Upload Pending','Code Review TA Completed','Code Review Completed','Documents Uploaded','Documents Reviewed by TechLead','Test case Updated','Document Review by TechLead Pending','Document Review by TechLead Pending','Developer Changed','TechLead Deleted','TechLead Changed','TechLead Added','Developer Deleted','TechLead Deleted','TechLead Changed','TechLead Added','Developer Deleted','TechLead Deleted','Initial Test Started')) pp where pp.request_id is not null )) p 
group by p.note_id) a on a.note_id = to_char(b.draft_no)
 left outer join mana0809.srm_request_assign@uatr_backup2 f on (f.request_id = e.request_id) 
 left outer join mana0809.emp_master@uatr_backup2 g on g.EMP_CODE = f.assign_to 
 left outer join (select max(r.target_date) tardt, r.request_id from mana0809.srm_request_assign@uatr_backup2 r group by r.request_id) s on f.request_id = s.request_id 
 left outer join mana0809.srm_software_request@uatr_backup2 u on b.draft_no = u.draft_id and u.request_id = e.request_id 
 left outer join mana0809.TBL_TRACKER_WORK_LOG@uatr_backup2 tt1 on tt1.note_id = to_char(b.draft_no) 
 left outer join mana0809.SRM_TECH_TEAM_LEAD@uatr_backup2 v on u.it_team = v.team_id and v.tech_lead = 1 
 left outer join mana0809.tbl_code_review@uatr_backup2 rv on rv.request_id=e.request_id 
 left outer join mana0809.emp_master@uatr_backup2 ep on ep.EMP_CODE=rv.assign_to 
 left outer join mana0809.emp_master@uatr_backup2 x  on x.EMP_CODE = v.emp_code left outer join (select distinct tm.type_id, tm.description as Module_Type from mana0809.srm_type_master@uatr_backup2  tm,  mana0809.srm_draft_master@uatr_backup2 dm  where dm.module_type = tm.type_id) yy
on yy.type_id = b.module_type left outer join (select a.request_id,  sum(a.no_of_changes * a.cost_change) as Total_Work_Hours  from mana0809.srm_manpower_calculator@uatr_backup2 a group by a.request_id) xxy on xxy.request_id = e.request_id left outer join (select wl3.note_id, max(wl3.received_date) as rec_date from mana0809.TBL_TRACKER_WORK_LOG@uatr_backup2 wl3 where wl3.sr_no = 2 and wl3.status = 'PMO Verification Pending'  group by wl3.note_id) wl2 on tt1.note_id = wl2.note_id left outer join (select ww.note_id, ww.received_date, ww.request_id from mana0809.tbl_tracker_work_log@uatr_backup2 ww where ww.sr_no = 20) wwl  on wwl.note_id = tt1.note_id and wwl.request_id = e.request_id where a.note_id = tt1.note_id and a.curr_status = tt1.updated_date and a.curr_status = tt1.updated_date and c.EMP_CODE = b.user_id and to_char(a.note_id) = to_char(b.draft_no) and b.dep_id = d.dep_id
  group by tt1.note_id,b.head_appr_date,e.request_id,e.development_manpower,ep.EMP_NAME,u.doc_update_sts,u.target_dt,b.priority,tt1.status,wwl.request_id,wwl.received_date,u.revised_date,b.note_id,b.tra_dt, b.objective,c.EMP_NAME,D.DEP_NAME,e.tl_name,b.note_app_dt,wl2.rec_date,b.target_dt,tt1.status,tt1.request_id,f.request_id,s.tardt,x.EMP_NAME,xxy.Total_Work_Hours,yy.Module_Type,b.status_id ) order by 1;

CRF tracker report for analysis 15-Jul-2022 start-- not correcct

 create table CRF_tracker_rpt as select distinct dd.crfid,
                dd.requestid,
                dd.requestdate,
                dd.projectname,
                dd.requestedby,
                dd.USERDEPRTMENT,
                dd.techlead,
                dd.TA_Completed_date,
                dd.developer,
                nvl(dd.test_engineer, dd.testername) as Test_engineer,
                dd.headapproved_date,
                dd.development_start_date,
                dd.development_complete_date,
                dd.testing_start_date,
                dd.test_end_date,
                nvl(dd.uat_assigned_date, to_char(woe1.received_date)) as uat_assigneddate,
                dd.user_targetdate,
                dd.TA_STARTDATE,
                dd.ta_targetdate,
                dd.project_target_date,
                dd.status,
                dd.RELEASE_DATE as user_confirm_date,
                dd.total_work_hours
  from (select distinct t.note_id CRFID,
                        e.request_id REQUESTID,
                        b.note_id APPROVALID,
                        to_char(b.tra_dt) REQUESTDATE,
                        b.objective PROJECTNAME,
                        c.EMP_NAME REQUESTEDBY,
                        D.DEP_NAME USERDEPRTMENT,
                        x.EMP_NAME TECHLEAD,
                        e.tl_name TA_COMPLETEDBY,
                        g.EMP_NAME AS DEVELOPER,
                        gg.EMP_NAME as test_engineer,
                        to_char(b.note_app_dt) MDAPPROVEDDATE,
                        to_char(b.head_appr_date) HEADAPPROVED_DATE,
                        nvl(to_char(www1.received_date),
                            to_char(wwww1.received_date)) as TA_Completed_date,
                        epp.EMP_NAME as testername,
                        to_char(min(ff.wokstart_dt)) as development_start_date,
                        to_char(max(ff.developer_update_dt)) as development_complete_date,
                        to_char(min(sta.workst_dt)) as Testing_Start_date,
                        to_char(max(sta.target_date)) as Test_End_date,
                        to_char(wo1.received_date) as UAT_assigned_date,
                        to_char(wq1.received_date) as UAT_confirmed_date,
                        to_char(b.target_dt) USER_TARGETDATE,
                        to_char(ff.tarstart_dt) as TA_STARTDATE,
                        to_char(s.tardt) TA_TARGETDATE,
                        nvl(to_char(u.target_dt), to_char(s.tardt)) PROJECT_TARGET_DATE,
                        case
                          when b.status_id in (99) then
                           decode(b.status_id, 99, 'CRF CANCELLED BY USER')
                          when nvl(upper(tt1.status), upper(t.status)) in
                               ('CRF EDITED', 'TECHLEAD HANDOVER') then
                           'TA PENDING'
                          else
                           nvl(upper(tt1.status), upper(t.status))
                        end STATUS,
                        --to_char(TT1.received_date) as User_confirmdate,
                        
                        to_char(wwl.received_date) RELEASE_DATE,
                        xxy.Total_Work_Hours ,
                        yy.Module_Type 
          from mana0809.emp_master@uatr_backup2       c,
               mana0809.department_mst@uatr_backup2   d,
               mana0809.srm_draft_master@uatr_backup2 b
          LEFT OUTER JOIN MANA0809.srm_techlead_status@uatr_backup2 E
            ON b.draft_no = E.DRAFT_NO
          left outer join (select p.note_id,
                                 p.request_id,
                                 max(p.updated_date) curr_status
                            from (select *
                                    from mana0809.tbl_tracker_work_log@uatr_backup2 tb
                                   where tb.status not in
                                         ('Documents Upload Pending',
                                          'Documents Uploaded',
                                          'Document Review by TechLead Pending',
                                          'Test case Updated',
                                          'Documents Reviewed by TechLead',
                                          'Code Review TA Completed',
                                          'Code Review Completed',
                                          'Developer Changed',
                                          'TechLead Deleted',
                                          'TechLead Changed',
                                          'TechLead Added',
                                          'Developer Deleted',
                                          'TechLead Deleted',
                                          'TechLead Changed',
                                          'TechLead Added',
                                          'Developer Deleted',
                                          'TechLead Deleted')) p
                           group by p.note_id, p.request_id) a
            on a.note_id = to_char(b.draft_no)
          left outer join mana0809.srm_testing@uatr_backup2 stt
            on (stt.request_id = e.request_id)
          left outer join mana0809.srm_test_assign@uatr_backup2 sta
            on (sta.request_id = stt.request_id)
          left outer join mana0809.emp_master@uatr_backup2 gg
            on gg.EMP_CODE = sta.assign_to
          left outer join mana0809.srm_request_assign@uatr_backup2 f
            on (f.request_id = e.request_id)
          left outer join mana0809.srm_request_assign@uatr_backup2 ff
            on (ff.request_id = e.request_id and ff.assign_to = f.assign_to)
        
          left outer join mana0809.emp_master@uatr_backup2 g
            on g.EMP_CODE = f.assign_to
          left outer join mana0809.POST_MST@uatr_backup2 O
            on G.POST_ID = O.POST_ID
          left outer join (select max(r.target_date) tardt, r.request_id
                            from mana0809.srm_request_assign@uatr_backup2 r
                           group by r.request_id) s
            on f.request_id = s.request_id
          left outer join mana0809.srm_software_request@uatr_backup2 u
            on b.draft_no = u.draft_id
           and e.request_id = u.request_id
          left outer join mana0809.TBL_TRACKER_WORK_LOG@uatr_backup2 t
            on to_char(b.draft_no) = to_char(t.note_id)
          left outer join mana0809.TBL_TRACKER_WORK_LOG@uatr_backup2 tt1
            on tt1.note_id = to_char(b.draft_no)
           and tt1.request_id = u.request_id
          left outer join mana0809.SRM_TECH_TEAM_LEAD@uatr_backup2 v
            on u.it_team = v.team_id
           and v.tech_lead = 1
          left outer join (select www.note_id, www.received_date, www.user_id
                            from mana0809.tbl_tracker_work_log@uatr_backup2 www
                           where www.sr_no = 30) www1
            on www1.note_id = t.note_id
           and www1.user_id = v.emp_code
          left outer join (select wwww.note_id,
                                 wwww.received_date,
                                 wwww.user_id
                            from mana0809.tbl_tracker_work_log@uatr_backup2 wwww
                           where wwww.sr_no = 7) wwww1
            on wwww1.note_id = t.note_id
           and wwww1.user_id = v.emp_code
          left outer join (select wo.received_date, wo.user_id, wo.request_id
                            from mana0809.tbl_tracker_work_log@uatr_backup2 wo
                           where wo.sr_no = 12) wo1
        --on wo1.note_id = t.note_id
            on wo1.request_id = u.request_id
           and wo1.request_id = e.request_id
          left outer join mana0809.emp_master@uatr_backup2 epp
            on epp.EMP_CODE = wo1.user_id
        --and wo1.user_id=sta.assign_to
          left outer join (select wq.note_id, wq.received_date, wq.user_id
                            from mana0809.tbl_tracker_work_log@uatr_backup2 wq
                           where wq.sr_no = 14) wq1
            on wq1.note_id = t.note_id
           and wq1.user_id = b.user_id
          left outer join mana0809.emp_master@uatr_backup2 x
            on x.EMP_CODE = v.emp_code
          left outer join (select distinct tm.type_id,
                                          tm.description as Module_Type
                            from mana0809.srm_type_master@uatr_backup2  tm,
                                 mana0809.srm_draft_master@uatr_backup2 dm
                           where dm.module_type = tm.type_id) yy
            on yy.type_id = b.module_type
          left outer join (select a.request_id,
                                 a.developer,
                                 sum(a.no_of_changes * a.cost_change) as Total_Work_Hours
                            from mana0809.srm_manpower_calculator@uatr_backup2 a
                           group by a.request_id, a.developer) xxy
            on xxy.request_id = e.request_id
           and xxy.developer = f.assign_to
        /*left outer join (select was.note_id, max(was.received_date)
        from mana0809.TBL_TRACKER_WORK_LOG was
        where was.sr_no = 22
        group by was.note_id)waq on waq.note_id=t.note_id */
          left outer join (select wl3.note_id,
                                 max(wl3.received_date) as rec_date
                            from mana0809.TBL_TRACKER_WORK_LOG@uatr_backup2 wl3
                           where wl3.sr_no = 2
                             and wl3.status = 'PMO Verification Pending'
                           group by wl3.note_id) wl2
            on t.note_id = wl2.note_id
          left outer join (select ww.note_id, ww.received_date, ww.request_id
                            from mana0809.tbl_tracker_work_log@uatr_backup2 ww
                           where ww.sr_no = 20) wwl
            on wwl.note_id = t.note_id
           and wwl.request_id = e.request_id
         where to_char(a.note_id) = to_char(t.note_id)
           and a.curr_status = t.updated_date
           and a.curr_status = tt1.updated_date
           and c.EMP_CODE = b.user_id
           and to_char(a.note_id) = to_char(b.draft_no)
           and b.dep_id = d.dep_id
           and tt1.sr_no = 20
           and to_DATE(TT1.received_date) > TO_DATE('30-jun-2022')
         group by t.note_id,
                  epp.EMP_NAME,
                  wwww1.received_date,
                  wo1.received_date,
                  wq1.received_date,
                  www1.received_date,
                  sta.target_date,
                  sta.workst_dt,
                  gg.EMP_NAME,
                  ff.tarstart_dt,
                  O.POST_NAME,
                  b.head_appr_date,
                  O.POST_ID,
                  g.EMP_NAME,
                  e.request_id,
                  FF.TARSTART_DT,
                  ff.target_date,
                  u.target_dt,
                  tt1.status,
                  wwl.request_id,
                  wwl.received_date,
                  b.note_id,
                  b.tra_dt,
                  b.objective,
                  c.EMP_NAME,
                  D.DEP_NAME,
                  e.tl_name,
                  b.note_app_dt,
                  wl2.rec_date,
                  b.target_dt,
                  t.status,
                  t.request_id,
                  f.request_id,
                  s.tardt,
                  x.EMP_NAME,
                  xxy.Total_Work_Hours,
                  yy.Module_Type,
                  b.status_id
         order by t.note_id) dd
  left outer join (select woe.received_date, woe.user_id, woe.request_id
                     from mana0809.tbl_tracker_work_log@uatr_backup2 woe
                    where woe.sr_no = 12) woe1
--on wo1.note_id = t.note_id
    on woe1.request_id = dd.requestid
 where dd.status not in ('CRF CANCELLED BY USER')
 order by 1 --left outer join mana0809.tbl_srm_feedback rr on rr.request_id=dd.REQUESTID order by 10"

1.create table PERSONAL_VISIT61 as
select t.branch_id,
       b.BRANCH_NAME,
       b.REG_NAME,
       b.AREA_NAME,
       t.emp_code,
       m.EMP_NAME,
       p.post_name,
       t.visit_dt,
       t.cust_name,
       t.cust_response,
       t.phone_no,
       t.enter_dt 
  from MANA0809.BR_PERSONAL_VISIT_NEW t,
       mana0809.emp_master            m,
       mana0809.branch_detail         b,
       mana0809.post_mst              p
 where t.emp_code = m.EMP_CODE
   and m.POST_ID = p.post_id
   and t.branch_id = b.BRANCH_ID
   and t.enter_dt  between '01-jun-2022' and '30-jun-2022' ;
---------
2.create table pv_new1 as select c.cust_id,
  --substr(c.cust_id, 1, 4) || '******' || substr(c.cust_id, 11, 14) cust_id,
         c.branch_id,
         t.branch_name,
         t.reg_name,
         t.area_name,
         t.emp_code,
         t.emp_name,
         t.post_name,
         t.visit_dt,
         t.cust_name,
         t.cust_response,
         t.enter_dt
    from mana0809.customer c, PERSONAL_VISIT61 t
   where (substr(c.phone2, -10) = substr(t.phone_no, -10) or
   substr(c.phone1, -10) = substr(t.phone_no, -10));

  3. select q.pledge_no,
   --substr(q.pledge_no, 1, 2) || '********' || substr(q.pledge_no, 11, 16) plno,
   q.pledge_val,
   q.act_weight,
   q.net_weight,
   q.stone_weight,
   q.scheme_nm,
   p.cust_id,
   --substr(p.cust_id, 1, 4) || '******' || substr(p.cust_id, 11, 14) cust_id,
   p.branch_id,
   p.branch_name,
   p.reg_name,
   p.area_name,
   p.emp_code,
   p.emp_name,
   p.post_name,
   p.visit_dt,
   p.cust_name,
   p.cust_response,
   p.enter_dt,
   to_date(d.reg_date) regdt,
   q.tra_dt pledge_dt,
   decode(g.status, 0, 'Settled', 'Live') inv_sts  from mana0809.pledge_master   q,
         mana0809.customer_detail d, 
         mana0809.pledge_status   s,mana0809.tbl_gln_inventory_master g,
       pv_new1                p 
   where q.cust_id = p.cust_id
     and d.cust_id = p.cust_id
     and s.pledge_no = q.pledge_no and s.inventory=g.inv_id
     and to_date(d.reg_date) >=p.enter_dt
     and q.tra_dt >= p.enter_dt ;

----------15-Jan-2022--------BCP /BCM---

****
MOR => Minimum Operating Requirements
MBCO => Minimum Business Continuity Objective
TTN => Total Time to Normalcy
IDR => Immediate Disaster Recovery
PC => Pre crisis Scenario
DC => During crisis scenario
RP=>
RTN => return to normal operations
MAO=> Maximum Acceptable Outage 
ORT
BCM => Bisuness Continuity Management
BAU => Business 
MAO=>
--Introduction-- start--
Objective & Scope						
The objective of functional BCP is to ensure recovery of critical processes within defined timelines. Scope includes following sites / facilities:			
						
Introduction						
Functional Plan: The functional plan for any function refers to the plan document which is vital in order to recover and resume the operations of the critical processes at a time of a crisis. It also reflects the importance of processes and their 'business continuity steps' in order to 'return to normal'. It even contains essential details of the vendors with the Immediate Disaster Response teams.										
						
Worksheet	Data 					
Critical Processes & Recovery Priority	Contains the list of Critical Processes for the Function					
MOR->MBCO	Contains the list of Critical Processes with their minimum operating requirements and vendor details					
MBCO->TTN	Contains the list of Critical Processes with their requirements to go from MBCO to TTN					
Function Name->PC	Contains the steps to be followed  during pre crisis scenario					
Function Name->DC	Contains the steps to be followed  during crisis scenario					
Function Name-RTN	Contains the steps to be followed to return to normal operations					
IDR	Contains the table of Process Owners and ORT					
Maximum Acceptable Outage (MAO)						
Minimum Business Continuity Objective (MBCO)	


----Introduction --- end--

select d.branch_name,b.remark,decode(t.access_id,'19','Normal Access','Privilaged Access') Access_ID,
                   t.discont_dt,
                   t.last_login,                 
                   to_date(t.last_login)-to_date(t.discont_dt)delaied_no_of_days,
                   c.dep_name,a.post_name,e.designation,
                   t.branch_id,
                   t.firm_id,
                   t.emp_code,
                   t.emp_name,
                   t.join_dt
                   from JJ t,post_mst a,status_mst b,department_mst c,branch_master d,designation_master e where e.designation_id=t.designation_id and d.branch_id=t.branch_id and c.dep_id=t.department_id and b.status_id=t.status_id and a.post_id=t.post_id
                   order by access_id desc;

---settled inventory data -- query from Shruthi (Archana PS) -- 18-Nov-2021---
select k.region_id,
       k.region_name,
       p.BRANCH_ID,
       p.BRANCH_NAME,
       t.audit_id,
       t.inv_no,
       t.issue_typ,
       t.irregularity,
       decode(t.rect_status, 1, 'Rectified', 2, 'Cannot be Rectified') Rect_Status,
       t.rect_bh_code,
       to_char(t.rect_date),
       t.rect_remarks,
       decode(m.priority_id,1,'low',2,'medium',3,'High',4,'Extreme','-')Priority
  from mana0809.TBL_DOC_settled_INVENTRY t,
       mana0809.audit_region_dtl         v,
       mana0809.audit_region_mst         k,
       mana0809.branch_dtl_new           p,
       mana0809.TBL_DOC_AUDIT_ISSUES     m
 where t.branch_id = v.branch_id
   and v.region_id = k.region_id
   and v.branch_id = p.BRANCH_ID
   and (t.irregularity not like '%Verified & Ok%' and
       t.irregularity not like '%No issue noticed%' and
       t.irregularity not like '%Not Applicable%' and
       t.irregularity not like '%Not applicable%')
   and t.spot_rect_st <> 1  and t.irregularity=m.issues(+) and t.fissue_typ_id=m.type_id(+) and t.class_id=m.class_id(+)
   and to_date(t.tra_dt) between '1-nov-2021' and '15-nov-2021';

----------From Kumar Ji on 18-Oct-2021 for Gl1 Gl2 ABH BH pledge approval for the selected list of pledge_nos----------
create table vidya_plno1 (pledge_no varchar2(16));
create index vidya_pl_no on vidya_plno1 (pledge_no);
select t.branch_id, 
       t.pledge_no,
       t.cust_name,
       t.cust_id,
       t.pledge_val,
       decode(s.status_id, 0, 'Settled', 'Live') plsts,
       decode(s.auction_id,
              0,
              'notauction',
              7,
              'underauction',
              8,
              'auctionsettled') auc_sts,
       r.user_id || e.EMP_NAME gl1,
       r.athority1 || em.EMP_name gl2,
       r.athority2 || ep.EMP_NAME abhorbh,
       r.athority3 || er.EMP_NAME bh,
       t.act_weight,
       t.net_weight,
       t.stone_weight
  from vidya_plno1 k
  left outer join mana0809.pledge_master t
    on (k.pledge_no = t.pledge_no)
  left outer join mana0809.pledge_status s
    on (k.pledge_no = s.pledge_no)
  left outer join mana0809.pledge_quot_his r
    on (k.pledge_no = r.pledge_no)
  left outer join mana0809.emp_master e
    on (e.EMP_CODE = r.user_id)
  left outer join mana0809.emp_master em
    on (em.EMP_CODE = r.athority1)
  left outer join mana0809.emp_master ep
    on (ep.EMP_CODE = r.athority2)
  left outer join mana0809.emp_master er
    on (er.EMP_CODE = r.athority3);

select t.branch_id emp_branch,t.emp_code,t.from_dt,t.to_dt,case when t.post_id=10 then 'BH' else 'ABH' end as BH_ABH,a.inv_id,a.cust_id,a.branch_id,a.plgno,a.close_dt

 where a.branch_id = t.branch_id

Red sticker data as  audited by Internal Auditor for the month perios 1-May to 15 May 2021 from backup db
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
select count(s.sticker_no), 
sum(a.net_weight) net_wt,
sum(a.act_weight) gr_wt,
       s.branch_id,
       b.BRANCH_NAME,
       b.REG_NAME,
     to_char(to_date(s.tra_dt), 'MON-YYYY')
      /* decode(s.item_id,
              0100600486,
              'red',
              0100600487,
              'green',
              0100600488,
              'blue',
              'others') colour*/
  from    goldloan_sticker_mst  s,   branch_detail b,pledge_master a
 where s.branch_id = b.BRANCH_ID
   and s.pledge_no is not null
   and s.item_id = 0100600486
   and s.status not in (3, 14, 15, 6, 4)
   and to_date(s.tra_dt) between '1-may-2021' and '17-may-2021' 
   and s.usr  in(select j.emp_code from   employee_master  j where j.department_id=4)
   and s.pledge_no=a.pledge_no
 group by s.branch_id,
          b.BRANCH_NAME,
          b.REG_NAME,
          to_char(to_date(s.tra_dt), 'MON-YYYY');
from Kumar Ji --Pledge Sticker status data query
--------------------------------------------------
select count(s.sticker_no), 
       s.branch_id,
       b.BRANCH_NAME,
       b.REG_NAME,
       to_char(to_date(s.tra_dt), 'MON-YYYY'),
       decode(s.item_id,
              0100600486,
              'red',
              0100600487,
              'green',
              0100600488,
              'blue',
              'others') colour
  from mana0809.goldloan_sticker_mst s, mana0809.branch_detail b
 where s.branch_id = b.BRANCH_ID
   and s.pledge_no is not null
   and s.status not in (3, 14, 15, 6, 4)
   and to_date(s.tra_dt) between '1-apr-2021' and '30-apr-2021'
 group by s.branch_id,
          b.BRANCH_NAME,
          b.REG_NAME,
          to_char(to_date(s.tra_dt), 'MON-YYYY'),
          S.ITEM_ID;

select t.pl_no,
       decode(s.status_id, 0, 'Settled', 'Live') plsts,
       case
         when m.status_id >= 11 and m.status_id < 16 then
          'auction_center'
         when m.status_id < 5 then
          'branch'
         when m.status_id > 5 and m.status_id <= 10 then
          'intransit'
         else
          'normal'
       end status
  from jj t,pledge_status s,auc_mst m -- m.>=11 and <16    <5 br
 where t.pl_no = s.pledge_no(+)
   and m.pledge_no(+) = t.pl_no

select a.slno || '^' || upper(c.descr) || '^' || a.user_id || '-' ||e.emp_name || '^' || to_date(a.request_dt) || '^' || d.descr || '^' ||a.objective || '^' || a.brief|| '^' || nvl(a.contact_no,'')|| '^' || nvl(a.emailid,'')|| '^' ||a.isattached || '^' || a.isattached2 || '^' || to_date(a.expect_dt) || '^' || CRF_ATTACHED,'Requet Id:' || a.slno || ' |Requested By:' || e.emp_name || ' | Module:' || upper(c.descr) ||' | Work:' || d.descr from mis.EMI_SCHEDULE a,department_mst b,COMMON_CONTROLS c,COMMON_CONTROLS d,employee_master e where e.department_id = b.dep_id  and a.status_id in (0,18,21) and c.module_id = 999 and c.param_id = 1 and a.module_id = c.status_id and d.module_id = 999 and d.param_id = 2 and a.work_type = d.status_id and a.user_id = e.emp_code and exists (select req_user from mis.emi_department t where a.user_id=t.req_user and t.app_user=323435) order by  slno)

ISMS- Change M Policy -- 2019 7304 12-Jun-2019 eff. date

1. BRS--The business team shall prepare a Business Requirement Specifications( Page 2 Point No#3)

2. CRF--The IT Department shall prepare the Change Request Form (CRF) for both application and IT infrastructure changes, and the document must also include fallback procedures along with the rollback actions. ( Page 2 Point No#4)

3. Risk Rating, cost and working hours -- An assessment should be performed to identify the potential impact including the information security impact, based on which the BRS and CRF shall be assigned a risk rating and classification based on the internal assessment. Once this activity is completed, the estimated cost and working hours are identified and recorded in the document.  ( Page 2 Point No#5)

4. CRB approval with IS requirements-- The BRS and CRF shall be approved, along with the verification of information security requirements, by the Change Advisory Board. ( Page 2 Point No#6)

5. High /Medium risk approval from HOD Risk--required  For all normal and emergency changes, if the risk rating is High and Medium an approval shall be obtained from the Head of Risk Department. ( Page 2 Point No#7)


6. Change ticket-- For all changes, a change ticket shall be raised in the centralized helpdesk tool. ( Page 2 Point No#10)

7. Testing & roll out to production --Once the change is developed and tested, the change shall be pushed to the production environment only once the approval from the Chief Technology Officer (CTO) or an equivalent personnel is obtained.

8. Change Implementation Plan (Page 4. Point #1)
   A change Implementation Plan shall be prepared for all normal changes.

9.  The Change Implementation Plan document may contain the following details: (Page 4. Point #2)
 Time and resource requirements
 Change impact description
 Change priority description
 Pre-requisites
 Test plan
 Implementation plan
 Technical group accountable for the change
 Change Type

9. Testing-- The changes shall be tested in the test environment as per the defined implementation plan, and the changes shall be pushed to production once the testing is successful.

10. Approval for emergency Changes CTO/ED: All emergency changes shall be approved verbally by the appropriate IT Functional Head before the implementation. This communication shall be recorded electronically by the change manager. These documents shall be verified by the Chief Technology Officer (CTO) or Executive Director (ED) while approving an emergency change.(Page 4. Point #4)

11. Review of Change CAB--All changes developed shall be submitted to the Change Advisory Board (CAB) for review (Page 4. Point #1)


12. Weekly CAB review : (Page 4. Point #2)
The Change Advisory Board shall conduct review meetings on a weekly basis. The meetings shall be attended by:
 Chief Technology Officer (CTO);
 Chief Information Security Officer (CISO);
 IT Functional Heads from application and infrastructure;
 Business Representatives;
 Subject Matter Experts (SME).

13. The Change Advisory Board shall review the effectiveness of changes based on the following parameters (but not limited to): (Page 5 Point no. #3)
 Changes achieving desired objective;
 Adherence to implementation plan;
 Clashing with other major changes;
 Unavailability of required subject matter experts.

14. The Change Advisory Board shall ensure that ineffective changes are rolled back. (Page 5 Point no #4)

15. Post implementation Review shall be recorded in Change ticket:
Change Management process requires that all implemented changes are reviewed for successful completion and to ensure that there has not been any adverse effect to the IT environment; and the Change Request ticket needs to be closed confirming the same. Sign-off from the business shall also be obtained, wherever applicable. Post-implementation review shall be performed for all deployed or attempted changes. The results of post-implementation review shall be recorded in the change ticket.


16. Retention Requirements:(Page 5 Point no. 1). The IT Department shall retain the change records, test plan and results and implementation plans for all changes and post-implementation review documents as per MAFILs standard for data retention.

Change records,
test plan and results
implementation plan
implementation review documents

# implement the RBIA framework by March 31, 2022 in accordance with the Guidelines on Risk-Based Internal Audit provided in the enclosed
##the concerned NBFCs and UCBs may constitute a committee of senior executives with the responsibility of formulating a suitable action plan. The committee may address transitional and change management issues and should report progress periodically to the Board and senior management.

create table hr_br_emp21122020 as select t.emp_code,
       t.emp_name,
       t.branch_id,
       j.branch_name,
       j.area_name,
       j.reg_name,
       j.zonal_name,
       T.POST_ID,
       K.POST_NAME,
       l.dep_name,
       t.department_id,
       m.remark as emp_status,
       n.from_dt as last_tfr_from_dt,
       o.from_dt as last_promotion_from_dt,
       b.to_dt previous_tfr_enddt,b.branch_id previous_tfr_endbranch,c.sex
  from mana0809.employee_master@uatr_backup2   t,
       mana0809.branch_detail_new@uatr_backup2 j,
       mana0809.post_mst@uatr_backup2          k,
       mana0809.department_mst@uatr_backup2    l,
       mana0809.status_mst@uatr_backup2        m,
       mana0809.employ_transfer_dtl@uatr_backup2 n,
       mana0809.employ_promotion_dtl@uatr_backup2 o,
       mana0809.employ_transfer_dtl@UATR_BACKUP2 b,
       mana0809.employ_personal_dtl@UATR_BACKUP2 c
 where 
     t.emp_code=c.emp_code
    and b.emp_code=n.emp_code
    and b.to_dt is null
   and b.to_dt=n.from_dt-1 
    and o.emp_code=t.emp_code
    and o.to_dt is null
    and n.emp_code=t.emp_code
    and n.to_dt is null
   and m.status_id=t.status_id
   and t.department_id=l.dep_id
   and k.post_id = t.post_id
   and j.branch_id = t.branch_id
   and t.status_id not in (99, 3, 4, 5, 6, 9, 10)
   and t.department_id = 14
   and t.post_id IN(1, 10,53,621,695,-251)
   and t.emp_code not in (select h.emp_code
                            from MANA0809.TBL_HRM_EMP_RESIGN_MST@UATR_BACKUP2 h
                           WHERE h.status in (0, 1));

------Auditor norms Vs Actual------7-Dec-2020----- with current region and Previous job region --circular 7813
select m.region_name previous_tfr_region_nm,l.region_id previous_tfr_regionID, b.to_dt previous_tfr_enddt,b.branch_id previous_tfr_endbranch,c.sex,k.state_name,j.district_name,o.region_name emp_cur_region,i.branch_id emp_cur_br_id,i.branch_name,to_date(sysdate)-a.from_dt no_od_days_exp,h.state_name emp_state_name,g.district_name emp_district_name, d.post_office emp_post_office,d.pin_code emp_pin_code, a.from_dt, a.br_dist, a.*
     from mana0809.employ_transfer_dtl@UATR_BACKUP2 a,
          mana0809.employ_transfer_dtl@UATR_BACKUP2 b,
          mana0809.employ_personal_dtl@UATR_BACKUP2 c,
          mana0809.post_master@UATR_BACKUP2         d,
          mana0809.branch_master@UATR_BACKUP2       e,
          emp_mst07122020                           f,
          mana0809.district_master@UATR_BACKUP2  g,
          mana0809.state_master@UATR_BACKUP2 h,
           mana0809.branch_master@UATR_BACKUP2  i,
           mana0809.district_master@UATR_BACKUP2 j,
            mana0809.state_master@UATR_BACKUP2 k,
             mana0809.audit_region_dtl@uatr_backup2 l,
             mana0809.audit_region_mst@uatr_backup2 m,
              mana0809.audit_region_d8tl@uatr_backup2 n,
              mana0809.audit_region_mst@uatr_backup2 o
    where f.emp_code = c.emp_code
    and o.region_id=n.region_id
    and n.branch_id=i.branch_id
    and l.region_id=m.region_id
    and l.branch_id=b.branch_id
    and b.emp_code=a.emp_code
    and b.to_dt=a.from_dt-1
    and k.state_id=i.state_id
    and j.district_id=i.district_id
    and i.branch_id=a.branch_id
      and g.district_id=d.district_id
      and h.state_id=g.state_id
      and a.emp_code = f.emp_code
      and e.branch_id = a.branch_id
      and a.emp_code = c.emp_code
      and c.perm_pin = d.sr_number
      and c.emp_code = c.emp_code
      and c.emp_code = a.emp_code
     /*and a.emp_code = 21983*/
      and f.department_id in (4, 330)
   and f.post_id in (248, 309,-252)
   and a.status_id<>6
      and a.to_dt is null;

 mana0809.hrm_earlygoing_appl@uatr_backup2 e, mana0809.employee_master@uatr_backup2 em, mana0809.branch_dtl_new@uatr_backup2 bm, mana0809.department_mst@uatr_backup2 d, mana0809.employ_firm@uatr_backup2 ef

  from MANA0809.TBL_NLOAN_LOAN_MST t, mana0809.tbl_nloan_disbursement_dtl a
 where a.loan_id = t.loan_id and a.paymt_status is not null and t.status_id=1 group by a.loan_id

Query for Accrued Interest
select c.product_name,
       a.loan_no,
       a.customer_id,
       a.cust_name,
       a.loan_amt,
       b.interest_rate,
       b.last_tra_dt,
       b.tenure,
       a.debt_bal,
       a.loan_bal,
       a.loan_dt,
       a.accrued_int
  from loan_accrual a, loan_master b, product_master c
 where b.product_id = c.product_id
   and b.loan_id = a.loan_no


----

Overdue Report Query
select c.product_name,
       a.loan_no,
       a.customer_id,
       a.cust_name,
       a.debt_bal,
       a.emi,
       a.due_no,
       a.phone_no,
       a.loan_dt
  from loan_accrual a, loan_master b, product_master c
 where b.product_id = c.product_id
   and b.loan_id = a.loan_no
   and a.debt_bal > 0


----
Cheque Bounce Details Report.
We are not able to generate this report for the previous data's which entered in mafil lms.

select c.product_name,
       e.scheme_name,
       sum(decode(a.collection_status, '1', a.collection_amount, 0)) Cleared,
       sum(decode(a.collection_status, '0', a.collection_amount, 0)) Bounced,
       sum(decode(a.collection_status, '2', a.collection_amount, 0)) Pending
  from loan_collection_master a,
       loan_master            b,
       product_master         c,
       payment_mode           d,
       scheme_master          e
 where b.product_id = c.product_id
   and b.loan_id = a.loan_id
   and d.clearance_method = 1
   and d.payment_mode_id = a.instrument_id
   and e.scheme_id = b.scheme_id
 group by c.product_name, e.scheme_name


---

Disbusrement Report Query.
select t.loan_id,
       d.scheme_name,
       a.customer_id,
       a.customer_name,
       a.loan_amount,
       t.disbused_amount,
       b.loan_bal + b.debt_bal outstanding,
       b.emi,
       a.tenure,
       a.interest_rate,
       b.maturity_date,
       b.pdc_stock,
       c.tra_date application_date,
       e.emp_name
  from lms_los.disbursement_details t,
       lms_los.loan_master          a,
       lms_los.loan_accrual         b,
       lms_los.application_mst      c,
       lms_los.scheme_master        d,
       lms_los.employee_master      e
 where c.application_id = t.application_id
   and e.emp_code = c.enter_by
   and a.loan_id = b.loan_no
   and t.application_id = a.application_id
   and d.scheme_id = a.scheme_id;

select b.dep_name as Post_name,
       '100' as staff_norms,
       count(a.emp_code) as actual_count,
       100 - count(a.emp_code) as actual_shortage,
       (select count(z.emp_code)
          from staff_long_leave z, employee_master y
         where z.absent_days >= 10
           and z.emp_code = y.emp_code
           and y.status_id = 1
           and y.department_id = 23) as shortage_10days,
       (select nvl(count(q.emp_code), 0)
          from TBL_HRM_EMP_RESIGN_MST q, employee_master p
         where q.status in (0, 1)
           and p.status_id = 1
           and q.emp_code = p.emp_code
           and p.department_id = 23) as undernotice_period,
           (select case when (nvl( x.emp_cnt,0)-100)>0 then x.emp_cnt else 0 end employee_count from (select count(k.emp_code) emp_cnt from employee_master k where k.status_id=1 and k.department_id=23)x) as surplus
  from employee_master a, department_mst b
 where b.dep_id = a.department_id
   and a.status_id = 1
   and a.department_id = 23
 group by b.dep_name

e.branch_add4  working_state,e.branch_add3 as work_district,e.branch_add2 as work_town,e.pincode Work_pin 
from employ_personal_dtl t,post_master a,employee_master b,district_master c, state_master d
,branch_master e,status_mst f ,department_mst g,post_mst h,grade_master i where 
i.grade_id=b.grade_id and h.post_id=b.post_id and g.dep_id=b.department_id and f.status_id=b.status_id and e.branch_id=b.branch_id and d.state_id=c.state_id and
 c.district_id=a.district_id and b.status_id=1 and t.emp_code=b.emp_code and t.emp_code=332694 and a.sr_number=t.perm_pin

select t.department_id,count(*) Last_mnthend_emp
  from mana0809.employee_master         e,
       mana0809.post_mst            p,
       mana0809.employ_firm         f,
       MANA0809.EMPLOY_TRANSFER_DTL t
  left outer join branch_detail b
    on t.branch_id = b.BRANCH_ID
 where t.status_id = 8
   and e.EMP_CODE = f.emp_code
   and t.post_id = p.post_id
   and t.emp_code = e.EMP_CODE
   and trunc(sysdate, 'MM')-1  between t.from_dt and case
         when t.to_dt is null then
          to_date(sysdate)
         else
          t.to_dt
       end
   and t.department_id in (123,617,634,620,622,623,621,637,632,631,635) group by t.department_id

       t.branch_id,
       round(count(distinct t.cust_id) ) cust_count,

       round(sum(t.balance) / 10000000) os,
       28 reportid
  from TBL_OGL_REBATE_AVAIL_1 t
 where t.int_rate = '12'
 group by t.branch_id;

 where t.int_rate = '15'
   and not exists (select *
          from TBL_OGL_REBATE_AVAIL_1 p
         where t.cust_id = p.cust_id
           and p.int_rate = '12')
 group by t.branch_id;

select a.branch_id,a.cutomer_count3MNT_BACK,b.cutomer_count2MNT_BACK,c.cutomer_count1MNT_BACK,d.cutomer_count_cur_MNT,a.gold_wt_3MNT_BACK,b.gold_wt_2MNT_BACK,c.gold_wt_1MNT_BACK,d.gold_wt_cur_MNT,a.os_3MNT_BACK,b.os_2MNT_BACK,c.os_1MNT_BACK,d.os_cur_MNT
from (select t.branch_id,t.cutomer_count as cutomer_count3MNT_BACK,t.act_wt-t.stone_wt as gold_wt_3MNT_BACK,t.gl_outstand as os_3MNT_BACK  from TBL_OGL_LIVECUST_SUMMARY t where tra_dt='31-Aug-2019') a,
(select t.branch_id,t.cutomer_count as cutomer_count2MNT_BACK,t.act_wt-t.stone_wt as gold_wt_2MNT_BACK,t.gl_outstand as os_2MNT_BACK  from TBL_OGL_LIVECUST_SUMMARY t where tra_dt='30-Sep-2019') b,
(select t.branch_id,t.cutomer_count as cutomer_count1MNT_BACK,t.act_wt-t.stone_wt as gold_wt_1MNT_BACK,t.gl_outstand as os_1MNT_BACK  from TBL_OGL_LIVECUST_SUMMARY t where tra_dt='31-Oct-2019') c,
(select t.branch_id,nvl(count(t.cust_id ),0) as cutomer_count_cur_MNT,nvl(sum(t.net_wt),0) as gold_wt_cur_MNT,nvl(sum(t.balance),0) as os_cur_MNT from pledge_acrual t  group by  t.branch_id) d
where a.branch_id=b.branch_id and b.branch_id=c.branch_id and c.branch_id=d.branch_id

select t.br_id,
       t.branch,
       t.area,
       t.region,
       t.f_zone,
       '100' as Growth_Tar_Today,
       t.today_clossing - t.today_opening as Achivement,
       ((nvl((t.today_clossing - t.today_opening), z/ 100) * 100)/* as  'Persentage' */,
       case when (t.today_clossing - t.today_opening) <0 then 'Negative' when ((t.today_clossing - t.today_opening) / 100) * 100 >=100 then 'Achieved' else 'Positive' end
  AS status,'5' as NCA_TAR,t.nca as NCA_Achivement,
  t.ba_nca,(select (SELECT EXTRACT(DAY FROM LAST_DAY(SYSDATE)) num_of_days FROM dual)- (select count(*) from dual connect by level <= 5
group by trunc(next_day(trunc(sysdate,'mm')-1, 'sunday') + (level -1)*7,'mm') 
having count(*) > 1) FROM DUAL)*5 AS nca_TARGET
  from Temp_tbl_growth_source_data t;

NVL(t.total_disb_wt/1000,0)total_disb_wt,NVL(t.total_auction_wt/1000,0)total_auction_wt,((NVL(t.total_auction_wt/1000,0)*10)/100) as Target,NVL(t.reduction_wt/1000,0) reduction_wt,NVL(t.total_auction_wt/1000,0)-NVL(t.reduction_wt/1000,0) as BALANCE
/*t.reduct_wt_tot,t.total_disb_wt,t.*, t.rowid*/ from tbl_auction_reduct_prevmnth  t WHERE T.FZM='FZM-6';

take over loan query for /achievment 6-Aug-2019 --for tableau MIS report
create table takeover_MIS_Source
 (
BRanch_id number(5),
BRANCH_NAME varchar2(50) ,
AREA_NAME varchar2(40) ,
REGION_NAME varchar2(40) ,
F_ZONE varchar2(150) ,
Pl_cnt_day number,
Pl_amt_day number,
Pl_wt_day  number,
MTD_Pl_cnt  number,
MTD_Pl_amt number,
MTD_Pl_wt number,
MTD_yes_day_cnt  number,
MTD_yes_day_amt number
)
-1.---todays count --
select t.branch_id,
       nvl(sum(m.pledge_val), 0) pl_val,
      sum(t.takeover_amt) takeover_amt,
     sum(m.act_weight-m.stone_weight) gold_wt,
     count(m.pledge_no) as pl_cnt,
       sum(case
             when m.pledge_no is null then
              0
             else
              1
           end) pl_count
  from mana0809.TAKEOVERLOAN_MST t
  left outer join mana0809.pledge_quot m
    on (t.cust_id = m.cust_id and m.pledge_no is not null and trunc(m.quot_dt) = trunc(t.tra_dt) and
       t.branch_id = m.branch_id)
where trunc(t.tra_dt) = trunc(sysdate) 
group by t.branch_id;

-2.----for previous day's data---
sselect t.branch_id, 
       nvl(sum(m.pledge_val), 0) pl_val,
      sum(t.takeover_amt) takeover_amt,
      sum(m.act_weight-m.stone_weight) gold_wt,
      count(m.pledge_no) as pl_cnt,
       sum(case
             when m.pledge_no is null then
              0
             else
              1
           end) pl_count
  from mana0809.TAKEOVERLOAN_MST t
  left outer join mana0809.pledge_quot m
    on (t.cust_id = m.cust_id and trunc(m.quot_dt) = trunc(t.tra_dt) and
       t.branch_id = m.branch_id)
where trunc(t.tra_dt) = trunc(sysdate)-1 
group by t.branch_id
union all
select t.branch_id, 
       nvl(sum(m.pledge_val), 0) pl_val,
      sum(t.takeover_amt) takeover_amt,
      sum(m.act_weight-m.stone_weight) gold_wt,
      count(m.pledge_no) as pl_cnt,
       sum(case
             when m.pledge_no is null then
              0
             else
              1
           end) pl_count
  from mana0809.TAKEOVERLOAN_MST t
  left outer join mana0809.pledge_quot_his m
    on (t.cust_id = m.cust_id and trunc(m.quot_dt) = trunc(t.tra_dt) and
       t.branch_id = m.branch_id)
where trunc(t.tra_dt) = trunc(sysdate) -1
group by t.branch_id
-3.---for month to date data----
select t.branch_id, 
       nvl(sum(m.pledge_val), 0) pl_val,
      sum(t.takeover_amt) takeover_amt,
      sum(m.act_weight-m.stone_weight) gold_wt,
      count(m.pledge_no) as pl_cnt,
       sum(case
             when m.pledge_no is null then
              0
             else
              1
           end) pl_count
  from mana0809.TAKEOVERLOAN_MST t
  left outer join mana0809.pledge_quot m
    on (t.cust_id = m.cust_id and trunc(m.quot_dt) = trunc(t.tra_dt) and
       t.branch_id = m.branch_id)
where trunc(t.tra_dt) = trunc(sysdate)
group by t.branch_id
union all
select t.branch_id, 
       nvl(sum(m.pledge_val), 0) pl_val,
      sum(t.takeover_amt) takeover_amt,
      sum(m.act_weight-m.stone_weight) gold_wt,
     count(m.pledge_no) as pl_cnt,
       sum(case
             when m.pledge_no is null then
              0
             else
              1
           end) pl_count
  from mana0809.TAKEOVERLOAN_MST t
  left outer join mana0809.pledge_quot_his m
    on (t.cust_id = m.cust_id and trunc(m.quot_dt) = trunc(t.tra_dt) and
       t.branch_id = m.branch_id)
where trunc(t.tra_dt) between trunc(sysdate) - (to_number(to_char(sysdate,'DD')) - 1) and trunc(sysdate)
group by t.branch_id

Circular No: 7223  
April 3, 2019 
 
Effective leave management  Modification of Circular No: 7200 
 
Management is pleased to make the following amendments to the earlier circular on effective management (Circular no: 7200) as follows:  
1. Casual leave & sick leave will be credited to the leave account of employees on a monthly basis for all category of employees. The practice of releasing the entire leave credit at the beginning of the financial year is discontinued. However, the above restriction shall not be applicable for Earned leave. It shall continue to be credited at the beginning of the year itself 
2. Effective from April 1st, 2019, the maximum monthly leave that can be sanctioned for an employee by his/her HoD or leave approving authority shall not exceed four (4) numbers. Excess leave, if any, must be submitted to MD & CEO for his approval. The count of four nos shall include all types of leave, including loss of pay leave 
 
3. In the case of employees who are working in states other than their native state, upto three days may be lost in travel time, when they avail leave to go home. In such cases, they may be allowed to take more than 4 days in a stretch, provided that their total leave availed does not exceed 12 nos. (Twelve) in a quarter 
 
4. HRM will monitor the leave availing of employees on a quarterly basis. Salary may be blocked for employees availing more than 12 nos (all leave types combined) in a quarter. Explanation will be sought from the concerned employees. Salary will be released for them only after approval from MD & CEO 
 
5. Only one leave per month is permitted to employees who have not completed one year of service 
 
6. The present restriction for availing Earned leave  maximum of 5 times a year is discontinued. Earned leaves availed in excess of 5 no.s need to be sanctioned  by MD & CEO 
 
7. All leaves in excess of 30 days in the financial year shall be permitted only with the prior approval of MD & CEO 
 
As we are a bringing a restriction on the total no of leaves that can be availed per month, the following restrictions are removed: 
 
* Compensatory off availed will not be considered in the count of leaves.  
 
 * Clubbing of leaves shall be allowed 
 
These modifications in leave rules is effective from 1st April 2019 
 
 
 
  Vipin G S                                                                                                                                                Vice President (Compliance)                                                                         
----------------------------------
CIRCULAR No. 7200 
19th March 2019 
 
 
Sub: Effective leave management  discouraging excess leave taking 
 
In order to discourage the tendency to avail too many leaves, the following changes/ restrictions in availing of leave are being introduced with immediate effect: 
 
 
1. Casual leave & sick leave will be credited to the leave account of employees on a monthly basis for all category of employees. The practice of releasing the entire leave credit at the beginning of the financial year is discontinued. However, the above restriction shall not be applicable for Earned leave. It shall continue to be credited at the beginning of the year itself 
 
2. HRM shall monitor the leave availing of employees on a quarterly basis. Salary may be blocked for employees availing more than 12 leaves (all leave types combined) in a quarter. Explanation will be sought from the concerned employees. Salary shall be released for them only after approval from MD & CEO 3. Only one leave per month is permitted to employees who have not completed one year of service 4. The present restriction for availing Earned leave is discontinued 
 
5. All leaves in excess of 30 days in the financial year shall be permitted only with the prior approval of MD & CEO
